msg:The two-night stay for this short birthday trip was comfortable and good. The staff were all professional and courteous.
The room is clean and new. It is not too big but the appropriate division of areas makes the room not feel cramped.
The sheets are smooth but the pillows are a bit soft and not supportive enough
There is also a dressing table in the room, which is very convenient
The room cleaning staff was very attentive and did not clean up my habits.
But it‚Äôs not that it‚Äôs not clean. I‚Äôve stayed in many hotels and they will clean them.
This saves you having to put things away the way you are accustomed to when you get back to the hotel at night.

I really like the bright and bright hotel floors, which are full of aviation-themed airplane models.
Quite special and thoughtful

Compared with the basic floors and rooms, the decoration of the breakfast restaurant is generally a bit out of place. There are many styles. There are new styles for breakfast for two consecutive days. The taste is okay.
There are relatively few meat dishes, and even if they are available, they feel like they have been cooked for a long time and become dry. The Chinese ones are relatively fresh. There are 4 choices of egg dishes and porridge flavors!
But it would be nice if there were fewer styles and fresher food.
There are many restaurants/light food restaurants in the shopping mall opposite. If there is a next time, I probably won‚Äôt buy hotel breakfast. I can just stay up late and go out for brunch.

In addition, the hotel specially arranged birthday surprise decorations and cakes on the birthday.
Very thoughtful towel cake decoration üòÇ quite interesting

The overall CP value of the hotel is very high. Several major routes pass by the bus station outside. The transportation is convenient.
